							<h2 class="zox-s-title1">Gospel Music Finds a New Home: Church Xtra with SOG Precious Premieres on Starr 103.5 FM</h2>
						</a>
		</div><!--zox-art-title-->
		<p class="zox-s-graph">Accra, Ghana — June 2, 2025 — There’s a fresh wave in gospel broadcasting! On Sunday, June 1st, celebrated radio personality SOG Precious premiered...</p>
		<div class="zox-byline-wrap">
			<span class="zox-byline-name"><a href="https://90bars.com/author/roj/" title="Posts by Renard Opoku" rel="author">Renard Opoku</a></span><span class="zox-byline-date"><i class="far fa-clock"></i>June 4, 2025</span>
